The hotel has a strong sense of service, and the service from the front desk to the doorman is proactive and enthusiastic. The lobby is spacious and gorgeous, and the upgraded room for us is even more surprising. It is spacious and bright, with complete and new facilities. It is actually more beautiful than the picture, and there are welcome fruits. When we checked out, the front desk attendant Xiao Cai enthusiastically gave us a souvenir. In short, the two-day stay made us feel happy physically and mentally. If there are two small suggestions for shortcomings, the first is whether the breakfast dishes should be improved. name:Xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€7â€1â€1â€7
info:Boutique Room - with View (Double bed)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:12 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:I stayed in this hotel twice in 2016, leaving very good memories. After returning to Hong Kong, I stayed in other chain or resort hotels. After staying in a circle, I still missed the ecological environment of Shazhou Lake. I came back here again to play paddle board. To be honest, the decoration of nearly 10 years does not meet the principle of choosing a new hotel. I was a little nervous after booking, worried that the facilities would be outdated. I didn't expect surprises one after another: the hotel's lakeside trail has beautiful scenery, and the elastic running track is very friendly to running enthusiasts; bottled water placed at the exit of the elevator on the floor can meet the needs at any time; my family has high requirements for bedding, and I didn't see the introduction of mattresses and bedding in the hotel introduction. I was also worried that there would be no latex pillows. As a result, the King Koil mattress is matched with a feather mattress, and there is a special menu for guests to choose from; the bathroom sanitary ware is very well maintained, and the toilet has also been upgraded to a smart toilet; the buffet breakfast also has tofu pudding in a wooden barrel, and the Chinese breakfast products are very suitable for Chinese stomachs. In addition, the hotel called to inquire about the check-in requirements the day before check-in, meeting my requirements for different room types to be close to each other, and upgrading to a lake view room, which is an absolutely perfect check-in experience. When you come to Zhangjiagang, I strongly recommend Shazhou Lake Hotel. It is suitable for visiting relatives and friends and vacationing. It only takes half an hour to reach any scenic spot in Zhangjiagang.

The environment is very beautiful, the air is fresh, and the surrounding greenery is very good. It is very enjoyable to take a walk after dinner.
The hotel rooms are luxuriously decorated, spacious and bright, clean and tidy, sanitary, and well-equipped. Every day, waiters deliver fruits, which is very humane. Thumbs up! In addition, two Starbucks coffee coupons are given when you check in, which can be consumed in the lobby or packed, which is great! ğŸ‘
The catering is also very complete, with a large banquet hall and various private rooms. The breakfast is also very good, with Chinese and Western food, and a variety of varieties. There is also a zero-point restaurant that is also very good! The dining environment is very good, and the restaurant has large transparent glass windows, and you can see the beautiful scenery outside.
It is worth mentioning that the hotel also has a spacious parking lot and underground garage, which is very convenient for parking. It is free to travel back and forth at the front desk by taking a parking QR code, which is very convenient!
Overall, I am very satisfied and give a five-star rating!
